	id = KOM.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.1" }

	desc = KOM.1.d

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Accept her as an agent
		name = KOM.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 60
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KOM.2
				days = 1
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_stalina_influence_change = yes
	}
	option = { #She cannot be trusted
		name = KOM.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 40
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KOM.4
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Voz cuts ties
	id = KOM.8
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.8" }
	title = KOM.8.t
	desc = KOM.8.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_generic_sign_treaty2

	is_triggered_only = yes
	trigger = {
		has_country_leader = { character = KOM_Nikolai_Voznesensky ruling_only = yes }
	}

	option = {
		name = KOM.8.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMZhdanovFavors > 15 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.9
					days = 2
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMZhdanovFavors < 16 }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.10
					days = 2
				}
			}
		}
		set_country_flag = KOM_VOZNESENSKY_CUT_TIES
	}
}

country_event = { #The election process begins - violence at the polls
	id = KOM.172
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM.172" }
	title = KOM.172.t
	desc = KOM.172.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_WAL_bobbies_riot

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap = KOMCenterPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap = KOMLeftPower }
		set_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap = KOMCenterPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap = KOMRightPower }
		set_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap = KOMLeftPower }
		subtract_from_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap = KOMRightPower }
	}

	option = {
		name = KOM.172.a
		hidden_effect = {
			KOM_elect_the_president = yes
			#Centrist majority government
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMLeftPower }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMRightPower }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap > 10 }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap > 10 }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_DEM_MAJORITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.173
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Leftist majority government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMCenterPower }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < -14 }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap > 14 }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_LEFT_MAJORITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.174
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Rightist majority government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMCenterPower }
							check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < -14 }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap < -14 }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_RIGHT_MAJORITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.175
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Centrist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMLeftPower }
							check_variable = { KOMCenterPower > KOMRightPower }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
							NOT = {
								check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < 10 }
								check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < 10 }
							}
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_DEM_PLURALITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.176
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Leftist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMCenterPower }
							check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
							NOT = {
								check_variable = { KOMCenterLeftGap < -14 }
								check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap > 14 }
							}
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_LEFT_PLURALITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.177
					days = 7
				}
			}
			#Rightist plurality government
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						AND = {
							check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMCenterPower }
							check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
							NOT = {
								check_variable = { KOMCenterRightGap < -14 }
								check_variable = { KOMLeftRightGap < -14 }
							}
						}
						has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION_RIGHT_PLURALITY }
					}
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.178
					days = 7
				}
			}
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_DEM
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.176
						days = 7
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_COMMIE
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.177
						days = 7
					}
				}
				if = {
					limit = {
						AND = {
							has_country_flag = KOM_PRESIDENT_FASH
							has_game_rule = { rule = KOM_FIRST_ELECTION option = DEFAULT }
						}
					}
					country_event = {
						id = KOM.178
						days = 7
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = KOM.176.a
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = komi_friendship.18
				days = 3
			}
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMLeftPower > KOMRightPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.179
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOMRightPower > KOMLeftPower }
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM.180
					days = 3
				}
			}
			else = {
				random_list = {
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = KOM.179
							days = 3
						}
					}
					50 = {
						country_event = {
							id = KOM.180
							days = 3
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
		add_to_variable = { KOMCoupRisk = 1 }
		set_country_flag = KOM_POST_ELECTION
	}
}

				}
				random_list = {

						KOM_generate_random_event = yes
					}

					}
				}
			}

				}
				random_list = {

						KOM_generate_random_event = yes
					}
					30 = {

					}
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					check_variable = { KOM_komi_coup_random_event > 12 }
				}
				random_list = {
					60 = {
						KOM_generate_random_event = yes
					}

					}
				}

		name = KOM_unstable_victory.248.a

			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_false_info
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM_unstable_victory.249
					hours = 1
				}
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_true_info
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM_unstable_victory.250
					hours = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = KOM_unstable_victory.251
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

add_namespace = KOM_left_coups

country_event = { #Ponomaryov coup, appeal for united party
	id = KOM_left_coups.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM_left_coups.1" }
	title = KOM_left_coups.1.t
	desc = KOM_left_coups.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_KOM_committee_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Ask for more support from Suslov
		name = KOM_left_coups.1.a
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_suslov_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMLeftPowerTemp = 3 }
		KOM_left_power_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_low = yes
	}
	option = { #Make a stronger alliance with Zhdanov
		name = KOM_left_coups.1.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^1 = 0 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^1 = 2 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^1 = 1 }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOMLeftPowerTemp = 3 }
		KOM_left_power_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_zhdanov_influence_change = yes
	}
	option = { #Aid Bukharina
		name = KOM_left_coups.1.c
		set_temp_variable = { KOMLeftPowerTemp = 3 }
		KOM_left_power_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_bukharina_influence_change = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Repurposing the Republic's institutions
	id = KOM_left_coups.5
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM_left_coups.5" }
	title = KOM_left_coups.5.t
	desc = KOM_left_coups.5.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_KOM_congress_3

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #Trust them
		name = KOM_left_coups.5.a
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					has_country_flag = KOM_appealed_to_dems
				}
				country_event = {
					id = KOM_left_coups.6
					days = 1
				}
			}
			else = {
				country_event = {
					id = KOM_left_coups.7
					days = 1
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #Don't trust them
		name = KOM_left_coups.5.b
		hidden_effect = {
			country_event = {
				id = KOM_left_coups.8
				days = 1
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Locking down Syktyvkar
	id = KOM_centre_coups.298
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM_centre_coups.298" }
	title = KOM_centre_coups.298.t
	desc = KOM_centre_coups.298.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_KOM_syktyvkar_2

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = { #A curfew is a bad idea.
		name = KOM_centre_coups.298.a
		add_political_power = 50
		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = 5 }
		KOM_center_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMLeftPowerTemp = 1 }
		KOM_left_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOMRightPowerTemp = 3 }
		KOM_right_power_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		hidden_effect = {
			random_list = {
				50 = {

				}
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = KOM_centre_coups.299
						days = 4
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
	option = { #EScort them back to their homes.
		name = KOM_centre_coups.298.b
		add_political_power = 20
		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = 1 }
		KOM_center_power_change = yes
	}
	option = { #Triple the night patrols - arrest anyone out past dark.
		name = KOM_centre_coups.298.c
		add_political_power = -75
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_low = yes
	}
}

add_namespace = KOM_stalina_coups

country_event = {
	id = KOM_stalina_coups.300
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM_stalina_coups.300" }
	title = KOM_stalina_coups.300.t
	desc = KOM_stalina_coups.300.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_KOM_stalina_1

	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.300.a
		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = 3 }
		KOM_center_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_stalina_influence_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_low = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.300.b
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^4 = 1 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^4 = 0 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^4 = 2 }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = 5 }
		KOM_center_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_stalina_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_morozov_influence_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_med = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.300.c
		trigger = {
			NOT = {
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^3 = 1 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^3 = 0 }
				check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^3 = 2 }
			}
		}
		set_temp_variable = { KOMCenterPowerTemp = 5 }
		KOM_center_power_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_stalina_influence_change = yes
		set_temp_variable = { KOM_pop_temp = 3 }
		KOM_voznesensky_influence_change = yes
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_med = yes
	}
}

	id = KOM_stalina_coups.301

		}

	}
	option = { #Organize it organically.
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.301.b

			random_list = {
				50 = {
					country_event = {
						id = KOM_stalina_coups.304
						days = 2
					}
				}
				25 = {
					country_event = {
						id = KOM_stalina_coups.303
						days = 2
					}
				}
				25 = {
					country_event = {
						id = KOM_stalina_coups.302
						days = 2
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

country_event = { #Suslov - successful arrest!
	id = KOM_stalina_coups.307
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event KOM_stalina_coups.307" }
	title = KOM_stalina_coups.307.t
	desc = KOM_stalina_coups.307.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IBR_pide_arrest

	is_triggered_only = yes
	immediate = {
		set_variable = { KOM_start_pops^0 = 0 }
		hidden_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = {
					OR = {
						check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^2 = 0 }
						check_variable = { KOM_leader_status^2 = 1 }
						has_country_flag = KOM_Bukharina_Recovered
					}
				}
				hidden_effect = {
					KOM_Power_Vacuum = {
						promote_character = { ideology = communist_subtype }
					}
				}
			}
			else = {
				KOM_Svetlana_Bukharina = {
					promote_character = yes
				}
			}
		}
	}

	option = {
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.307.a
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		country_event = {
			id = KOM_stalina_coups.309
			days = 2
		}
		set_variable = { KOM_leader_status^0 = 1 }
		KOM_eliminate_left_leader = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = KOM_stalina_coups.307.b
		KOM_decrease_coup_risk_static_low = yes
		add_political_power = 25
		set_variable = { KOM_leader_status^0 = 1 }
		KOM_eliminate_left_leader = yes
	}
}

country_event = { #Overture to the Front
	id = komidiplo.1
	immediate = { log = "[GetDateText]: [Root.GetName]: event komidiplo.1" }
	title = komidiplo.1.t
	desc = komidiplo.1.d
	picture = GFX_report_event_IBR_filing_cabinet

	fire_only_once = yes
	is_triggered_only = yes

	option = {
		name = komidiplo.1.a
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 100
			modifier = {
				NOT = {
					has_government = socialist
					has_government = communist
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		KOM = {
			country_event = {
				id = komidiplo.2
				days = 3
			}
		}
	}
	option = {
		name = komidiplo.1.b
		ai_chance = {
			factor = 50			
			modifier = {
				AND = {
					OR = {
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = WRS_INTEGRATION_KOMI
							option = WRS_INTEGRATION_KOMI_YES
						}
						has_game_rule = {
							rule = WRS_INTEGRATION_KOMI
							option = WRS_INTEGRATION_KOMI_INTEGRATES_WRRF_YES
						}
					}
					OR = {
						has_government = socialist
						has_government = communist
					}
				}
				factor = 0
			}
		}
		KOM = {
			country_event = {
				id = komidiplo.3
				days = 3
			}
		}
		KOM = { set_country_flag = WRS_SOVKOM_WAR }
		WRS = { set_country_flag = WRS_SOVKOM_WAR }
	}
}

				ideology = national_socialism
				popularity = 1
			}
			add_popularity = {
				ideology = communist
				popularity = 0.5
			}
			set_capital = { state = 1613 }
			set_cosmetic_tag = CME_PACIFICA
			set_party_name = {
				ideology = national_socialism
				long_name = CME_shitpost_party
				name = CME_shitpost_party
			}
			#econtype
			set_temp_variable = { TNO_economy_subtype_temp = token:Econ_Subtype_Burgsys }
			econ_subtype_change = yes
		}
	}
